style="text-align:center"><font style="color:#4f2370;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:16pt;font-weight:700;line-height:112%">Mondel&#275;z International Appoints Cees &#8216;t Hart to Board of Directors</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:700;line-height:112%"> </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="text-indent:36pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:150%">CHICAGO, July 20, 2023</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:150%"> &#8211; Mondel&#275;z International, Inc. (Nasdaq&#58; MDLZ) today announced the appointment of Cees &#8216;t Hart to the Company&#8217;s Board of Directors, effective today.</font></div><div style="text-indent:36pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:150%">&#8220;We are pleased to welcome Cees to our Board. His deep experience building local and international brands makes him an invaluable resource for our company,&#8221; said Dirk Van de Put, Chairman &#38; CEO of Mondel&#275;z International.</font></div><div style="text-indent:36pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:150%">&#8216; t Hart has worked for more than 30 years in the food and beverage industry, most recently serving as CEO of Carlsberg Group, a position he&#8217;s held since 2015. Before joining Carlsberg, &#8216;t Hart was CEO of Royal FrieslandCampina. Previously, he held various positions within Unilever across Eastern and Western Europe as well as Asia. During his tenure at Unilever, he served as a member of the Europe Executive Board. &#8217;t Hart currently serves as Chairman of KLM's Supervisory Board and sits on the Board of AirFranceKLM.</font></div><div style="text-indent:36pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:150%">&#8216;t Hart&#8217;s appointment expands the size of the Company&#8217;s Board to 10 members.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#4f2170;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:700;line-height:150%">About Mondel&#275;z International</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:150%">Mondel&#275;z International, Inc. (Nasdaq&#58; MDLZ) empowers people to snack right in over 150 countries around the world. With 2022 net revenues of approximately $31 billion, MDLZ is leading the future of snacking with iconic global and local brands such as </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:150%">Oreo</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:150%">, </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:150%">Ritz, LU, Clif Bar</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:150%"> and </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:150%">Tate's Bake Shop</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:150%"> biscuits and baked snacks, as well as </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:150%">Cadbury Dairy Milk</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:150%">, </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:150%">Milka</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:150%"> and </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:150%">Toblerone</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:150%"> chocolate. Mondel&#275;z International is a proud member of the Standard and Poor&#8217;s 500, Nasdaq 100 and Dow Jones Sustainability Index. Visit </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:150%;text-decoration:underline">www.mondelezinternational.com</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:150%"> or follow the company on Twitter at </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:150%;text-decoration:underline">www.twitter.com&#47;MDLZ</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:150%">.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#4f2170;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:700;line-height:150%">Forward-Looking Statements</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:150%">This press release contains forward-looking statements.
